  ---
  SECTION V-B: UPLINK DATA TRANSMISSION (Scalable Combining Schemes)

  Paper: "Scalable Cell-Free Massive MIMO Systems" вҖ” BjГ¶rnson & Sanguinetti 
  (2020)

  (Second part of Section V. Covers centralized combining (Proposition 1, MR, 
  MMSE, P-MMSE) and distributed combining (Proposition 2, LP-MMSE, Corollary 
  2).)

  ---
  1. HIGH-LEVEL EXPLANATION (Layman's Terms)

  When many people talk at the same time in a room (uplink), the listeners (APs)
   hear everyone's voices mixed together. Combining is the technique the
  listeners use to focus on one specific speaker and tune out the others.

  There are two approaches to this:

  Centralized combining: All the listeners record what they hear and send the
  raw recordings to a central office. The office, having all the recordings,
  uses sophisticated math to figure out what each speaker said. This is very
  accurate but requires sending massive amounts of data (recordings) to the
  central office.

  Distributed combining: Each listener does their own basic processing locally вҖ”
   they partially figure out what the nearby speaker said вҖ” and only send a
  short summary (a single number) to the central office. The office combines
  these summaries. This needs way less data transfer but is slightly less
  accurate.

  Within each approach, there are different "quality levels" of listening:

  - MR (Maximum Ratio): The simplest вҖ” just amplify the direction where you
  expect the speaker to be. Ignores other speakers completely. Cheap but
  mediocre.
  - MMSE: The best possible вҖ” simultaneously amplifies the desired speaker AND
  suppresses all interfering speakers. Expensive (requires knowing about ALL
  speakers) and unscalable.
  - P-MMSE (Partial MMSE): The clever compromise вҖ” suppress only the interfering
   speakers that share your same listeners. Ignores distant speakers who don't
  affect you much. Nearly as good as full MMSE but scalable.
  - LP-MMSE (Local P-MMSE): The distributed version вҖ” each listener locally does
   the P-MMSE trick using only their own knowledge. Even cheaper and still
  scalable.

  ---
  2. DETAILED TECHNICAL EXPLANATION (PhD Level)

  2.1 Two Levels of Cooperation

  The paper considers two levels of cooperation among APs for UL data decoding:

  Level 1 вҖ” Centralized combining: AP l sends its raw received pilot signals
  {yвӮңвӮ—бө–вҒұЛЎбө’бө— : t = 1,...,П„вӮҡ} and raw data signal yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ to the CPU through the
  fronthaul link. The CPU performs both channel estimation and data detection.

  Level 2 вҖ” Distributed combining: AP l locally estimates channels {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ
  рқ’ҹвӮ—} and locally computes soft estimates vвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ. Only these scalar soft
  estimates are sent to the CPU, which sums them for final decoding.

  Fronthaul comparison (from Table I in the paper):

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ   Signal Type   в”Ӯ  Centralized  в”Ӯ   Distributed    в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Pilot signals   в”Ӯ П„вӮҡ N scalars  в”Ӯ вҖ” (not sent)     в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ UL data signals в”Ӯ П„бөӨ N scalars  в”Ӯ П„бөӨ |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ DL data signals в”Ӯ П„_d N scalars в”Ӯ П„_d |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Centralized fronthaul per AP per coherence block: (П„вӮҡ + П„бөӨ) Г— N complex
  scalars.
  Distributed fronthaul per AP per coherence block: П„бөӨ Г— |рқ’ҹвӮ—| complex scalars.

  Under Assumption 1, |рқ’ҹвӮ—| вүӨ П„вӮҡ, so the distributed fronthaul is bounded by П„бөӨ Г—
   П„вӮҡ вҖ” independent of K and typically much smaller than the centralized
  requirement (especially when N is large).

  2.2 Centralized Combining вҖ” Proposition 1

  In the centralized case, the CPU has access to all channel estimates and can
  form the collective combining vector vвӮ– вҲҲ в„Ӯбҙёбҙә for UE k.

  Partial knowledge of estimates: Under DCC, the CPU only knows the channel
  estimates from APs that send their pilot signals. Specifically, the CPU knows:

  в–Һ Dбөў ДҘбөў = [DбөўвӮҒ ДҘбөўвӮҒбөҖ  ...  DбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бөҖ]бөҖ        ... (Eq. 16)

  where unknown estimates (from APs not serving UE i) are represented by zeros.
  The distribution:

  в–Һ Dбөў ДҘбөў ~ рқ’©б¶ң(0, pбөў П„вӮҡ Dбөў Rбөў ОЁвӮңбөўвҒ»В№ Rбөў Dбөў)

  Also define the collective estimation error:

  в–Һ hМғбөў = hбөў вҲ’ ДҘбөў ~ рқ’©б¶ң(0, Cбөў)

  where Cбөў = diag(CбөўвӮҒ, ..., CбөўвӮ—) and CбөўвӮ— = RбөўвӮ— вҲ’ pбөў П„вӮҡ RбөўвӮ— ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№ RбөўвӮ— (the error
   covariance).

  Proposition 1 вҖ” Achievable UL SE (Centralized)

  в–Һ An achievable SE of UE k is:

  в–Һ SEвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = (П„бөӨ / П„б¶ң) рқ”ј{logвӮӮ(1 + SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ)}        ... (Eq. 17)

  в–Һ where the instantaneous effective SINR is:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = pвӮ– |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ / (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· pбөў |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘбөў|ВІ + vвӮ–бҙҙ ZвӮ– vвӮ–)     
     ... (Eq. 18)

  в–Һ with ZвӮ– = DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў Cбөў + ПғВІ IвӮ—вӮҷ) DвӮ–

  Dissecting the SINR expression (Eq. 18):

  Numerator: pвӮ– |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ
  - This is the desired signal power after combining
  - DвӮ– masks out APs not serving UE k
  - ДҘвӮ– is the known channel estimate
  - The combining vector vвӮ– projects the signal onto UE k's direction

  Denominator вҖ” Term 1: вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· pбөў |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘбөў|ВІ
  - Interference from estimated channels of other UEs
  - Only UEs whose estimates are known at APs serving UE k contribute nonzero
  terms
  - This is the interference the CPU can potentially suppress (it knows these
  estimates)

  Denominator вҖ” Term 2: vвӮ–бҙҙ ZвӮ– vвӮ–
  - This captures estimation errors and noise
  - ZвӮ– = DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөў pбөў Cбөў + ПғВІ I) DвӮ– includes:
    - вҲ‘бөў pбөў Cбөў : interference from the unknown parts of all channels (estimation
   errors)
    - ПғВІ I : thermal noise

  Key property: This SE expression holds for any combining vector vвӮ–, any
  spatial correlation matrices, and any DCC configuration вҖ” it is a general
  result.

  Source: The proof follows [2, Th. 4.1] for Massive MIMO.

  2.3 MR Combining in the Centralized Case (Equation 19)

  The simplest combining choice:

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙ№бҙҝ = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 19)

  The DвӮ– ensures that only APs serving UE k contribute (ДҘвӮ–вӮ— is zeroed out for l
  вҲү в„івӮ–). Since DвӮ–вӮ— = 0вӮҷ implies DвӮ–вӮ— ДҘвӮ–вӮ— = 0, only the MMSE estimates at APs in
  в„івӮ– are needed.

  Complexity (from Table II): Channel estimation requires (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ) |в„івӮ–|
  multiplications. The combining vector computation requires no additional
  multiplications (it IS the estimate). Scalable since |в„івӮ–| is bounded.

  Drawback: MR maximizes the numerator |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ of Eq. (18) but completely
  ignores the denominator (interference + noise). It does nothing to suppress
  interference.

  2.4 MMSE Combining вҖ” Optimal but Unscalable (Equation 20, Corollary 1)

  The paper observes that Eq. (18) has the form of a generalized Rayleigh 
  quotient with respect to vвӮ–. This is a classic optimization problem in linear
  algebra.

  Generalized Rayleigh Quotient: For matrices A вүҪ 0 and B вү» 0:

  в–Һ max_v (vбҙҙ A v) / (vбҙҙ B v)

  is achieved by v = BвҒ»В№ a (or BвҖ  a if B is singular), where a is the principal
  eigenvector of BвҒ»В№ A. When A = a****aбҙҙ is rank-1, the maximum is aбҙҙ BвҒ»В№ a.

  Applying this to Eq. (18): The SINR is:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ– = pвӮ– |vвӮ–бҙҙ (DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–)|ВІ / (vвӮ–бҙҙ [вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–] vвӮ–)

  This is a generalized Rayleigh quotient with:
  - a = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– (numerator direction)
  - B = вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ– (denominator matrix)

  Corollary 1: The SINR-maximizing combining vector is:

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 20)

  yielding the maximum SINR:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = pвӮ– ДҘвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... 
  (Eq. 21)

  Derivation of Eq. (20):

  Starting from the generalized Rayleigh quotient [2, Lemma B.10]:

  в–Һ v_opt = c В· BвҖ  a     (c is any non-zero scalar)

  where a = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– and B = вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–.

  Note that the desired signal term can be moved into the denominator matrix:

  в–Һ B' = вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ– = B + pвӮ– DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– ДҘвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ–

  Using the matrix inversion lemma (or directly), vвӮ– = pвӮ– (B')вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– gives the
  same SINR-maximizing direction.

  Why MMSE? The combiner in Eq. (20) also minimizes the conditional MSE:

  в–Һ MSEвӮ– = рқ”ј{|sвӮ– вҲ’ ЕқвӮ–|ВІ | {ДҘбөў}}

  between the data signal sвӮ– and the received signal ЕқвӮ– in Eq. (9) вҖ” hence the
  name MMSE combining.

  The scalability problem: Eq. (20) requires computing the channel estimates
  {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i = 1,...,K} at every AP l that serves UE k. The matrix to invert has
  size N|в„івӮ–| Г— N|в„івӮ–|, but it sums over ALL K UEs. From Table II:

  в–Һ Complexity вҲқ (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ K + (N|в„івӮ–|)Ві

  The K factor makes this unscalable as K вҶ’ вҲһ.

  2.5 P-MMSE Combining вҖ” The Scalable Innovation (Equations 22вҖ“24)

  This is one of the paper's key contributions. The insight comes from [30]: the
   interference affecting UE k is mainly generated by a small subset of other
  UEs вҖ” specifically, those served by partially the same APs.

  Define the set рқ’«вӮ– (Equation 22):

  в–Һ рқ’«вӮ– = {i : DвӮ– Dбөў вү  0вӮ—вӮҷ}        ... (Eq. 22)

  Physical meaning: рқ’«вӮ– contains all UEs that share at least one AP with UE k.
  These are the UEs whose interference most strongly affects UE k, because they
  are beamformed from the same APs.

  Example: If UE k is served by APs {2, 5, 7}, and:
  - UE 3 is served by APs {5, 8} вҶ’ DвӮ– DвӮғ вү  0 (overlap at AP 5) вҶ’ 3 вҲҲ рқ’«вӮ–
  - UE 6 is served by APs {1, 9} вҶ’ DвӮ– DвӮҶ = 0 (no overlap) вҶ’ 6 вҲү рқ’«вӮ–

  UE 6 does cause interference to UE k (radio waves still propagate), but this
  interference:
  1. Is not beamformed toward UE k's APs
  2. Is captured by the Z'вӮ– term (treated statistically as noise)
  3. Has relatively small impact

  The P-MMSE combining vector (Equation 23):

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + Z'вӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 23)

  with the modified noise-plus-interference covariance:

  в–Һ Z'вӮ– = DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮ– pбөў Cбөў + ПғВІ IвӮ—вӮҷ) DвӮ–        ... (Eq. 24)

  Compare P-MMSE (Eq. 23) with full MMSE (Eq. 20):

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ                 в”Ӯ Full MMSE (Eq. 20) в”Ӯ       P-MMSE (Eq. 23)        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Summation range в”Ӯ вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· (all K UEs)  в”Ӯ вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮ– (only overlapping UEs) в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Matrix size     в”Ӯ N|в„івӮ–| Г— N|в„івӮ–|      в”Ӯ N|в„івӮ–| Г— N|в„івӮ–| (same)         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Number of terms в”Ӯ K                  в”Ӯ |рқ’«вӮ–|                         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Depends on K?   в”Ӯ Yes вҶ’ unscalable   в”Ӯ No вҶ’ scalable вң…             в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Bounding |рқ’«вӮ–|:

  The paper proves that |рқ’«вӮ–| is bounded independent of K:

  - If all APs serving UE k communicate with exactly the same set of UEs: |рқ’«вӮ–| =
   П„вӮҡ
  - In the worst case (each AP in в„івӮ– serves entirely different UEs except UE k):
   |рқ’«вӮ–| вүӨ (П„вӮҡ вҲ’ 1)|в„івӮ–| + 1

  Both bounds are independent of K since П„вӮҡ and |в„івӮ–| are both bounded constants.

  Complexity (from Table II):

  в–Һ P-MMSE: (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ |рқ’«вӮ–|/2 + (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ + (N|в„івӮ–|)Ві вҲ’ N|в„івӮ–|/3

  All terms are independent of K вҶ’ scalable вң…

  When does P-MMSE coincide with MMSE? When UE k is served by all APs (i.e., DвӮ–
  = IвӮҳ), then рқ’«вӮ– includes all K UEs (every UE shares at least one AP with k),
  and P-MMSE = MMSE. But in that case, neither is scalable.

  2.6 Distributed Combining вҖ” Proposition 2

  In the distributed case, each AP locally processes its received signal. AP l:
  1. Computes local estimates {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—}
  2. Selects combining vector vвӮ–вӮ— based on these local estimates
  3. Computes the local soft estimate (Equation 25):

  в–Һ ЕқвӮ–вӮ— = vвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ DвӮ–вӮ— yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ        ... (Eq. 25)

  4. Sends ЕқвӮ–вӮ— to the CPU

  The CPU forms the final estimate by summing (Equation 26):

  в–Һ ЕқвӮ– = вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё ЕқвӮ–вӮ—        ... (Eq. 26)

  Fronthaul load: AP l sends |рқ’ҹвӮ—| complex scalars per UL time slot (one per
  served UE). Over the entire UL phase: П„бөӨ |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars per coherence block.
  Under Assumption 1, this is bounded by П„бөӨ П„вӮҡ вҖ” scalable.

  The SE challenge: Since the CPU does NOT have the channel estimates in the
  distributed case, the SE cannot be computed as in Proposition 1. Instead, the
  paper uses the Use-and-then-Forget (UatF) bound.

  Proposition 2 вҖ” Achievable UL SE (Distributed)

  в–Һ An achievable UL SE for UE k is:

  в–Һ SEвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ = (П„бөӨ / П„б¶ң) logвӮӮ(1 + SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ)        ... (Eq. 27)

  в–Һ where:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ = pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ / (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} вҲ’ pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– 
  hвӮ–}|ВІ + ПғВІ рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ})        ... (Eq. 28)

  Dissecting the SINR (Eq. 28):

  Numerator: pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ
  - The average desired signal power вҖ” based only on the statistical mean of the
   effective channel
  - The UE decodes using рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–} as the known effective channel gain

  Denominator:
  - вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} : average total power (desired + all interference +
   estimation error effects)
  - вҲ’ pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ : subtract the desired signal term (moved to numerator)
    - ПғВІ рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ} : noise term

  Key difference from Proposition 1: In Proposition 1 (centralized), the SINR is
   instantaneous вҖ” it depends on the actual channel realizations (ДҘбөў), and the
  SE involves an expectation over these realizations (Eq. 17). In Proposition 2
  (distributed), the SINR is deterministic вҖ” all randomness is averaged out
  through the expectations in Eq. (28). The log is outside the expectation вҖ” no
  need for Monte Carlo averaging over channel realizations (though the
  expectations themselves may require it).

  Why the UatF bound? The CPU in the distributed case only receives the scalar
  ЕқвӮ– = вҲ‘вӮ— ЕқвӮ–вӮ—. It does NOT know the instantaneous effective channel vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ– вҖ”
  only its statistical mean рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}. The UatF technique treats this mean as
   the known "channel" and everything else (channel fluctuations, interference)
  as worst-case Gaussian noise. This gives a conservative but achievable SE.

  2.7 LP-MMSE Combining вҖ” The Scalable Distributed Scheme (Equation 29)

  For distributed combining, each AP must independently select its combining
  vector. The paper proposes Local Partial MMSE (LP-MMSE):

  в–Һ vвӮ–вӮ—бҙёбҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ)вҒ»В№ ДҘвӮ–вӮ—        ... (Eq. 
  29)

  Let me break this down term by term:

  The matrix being inverted: вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ

  - ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ : the outer product of the channel estimate вҖ” represents the known
  part of UE i's interference
  - CбөўвӮ— : the estimation error covariance вҖ” represents the unknown part of UE
  i's channel
  - Together: ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ— вүҲ рқ”ј{hбөўвӮ— hбөўвӮ—бҙҙ | ДҘбөўвӮ—} (the conditional covariance of
  the true channel)
  - Sum over i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ— : only UEs served by AP l вҖ” not all K UEs!
    - ПғВІ IвӮҷ : noise

  The right-hand side: ДҘвӮ–вӮ— вҖ” the local estimate of UE k's channel

  Physical interpretation: LP-MMSE at AP l inverts a local
  "interference-plus-noise covariance" that includes only the UEs this AP
  serves, then projects onto the desired UE's estimated channel direction. It is
   a local Wiener filter.

  Key difference from L-MMSE [7]: L-MMSE (introduced in BjГ¶rnson & Sanguinetti
  2020 [7]) sums over ALL K UEs:

  в–Һ vвӮ–вӮ—бҙёвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ)вҒ»В№ ДҘвӮ–вӮ—

  The only difference: L-MMSE sums over i = 1,...,K while LP-MMSE sums over i вҲҲ
  рқ’ҹвӮ—. Since |рқ’ҹвӮ—| вүӨ П„вӮҡ, LP-MMSE is scalable while L-MMSE is not.

  Complexity (from Table II): Per UE k at each AP l вҲҲ в„івӮ–:

  в–Һ (NВІ + N)/2 Г— |рқ’ҹвӮ—| + (NВі вҲ’ N)/3 + NВІ

  - Matrix construction: (NВІ + N)/2 per UE in рқ’ҹвӮ— вҶ’ scales with |рқ’ҹвӮ—| (bounded by
  П„вӮҡ)
  - Matrix inversion: O(NВі) вҖ” only an N Г— N matrix! (vs. N|в„івӮ–| Г— N|в„івӮ–| for
  centralized P-MMSE)
  - Total: O(П„вӮҡ NВІ + NВі) per AP вҖ” independent of K вң…

  Why LP-MMSE vastly outperforms MR: Even though LP-MMSE uses only local CSI,
  it:
  1. Suppresses local interference spatially (when N > 1)
  2. Reduces effective channel gain variations вҖ” the SINR becomes more
  predictable, improving the tightness of the UatF bound
  3. Achieves SE improvements of 2вҖ“3Г— over MR in typical scenarios

  2.8 Corollary 2 вҖ” Closed-Form SE with MR Combining

  When MR combining (vвӮ–вӮ— = ДҘвӮ–вӮ—) is used, the expectations in Eq. (28) can be
  computed in closed form. The paper derives (Corollary 2):

  Desired signal (Equation 30):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–} = pвӮ– П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)        ... (Eq. 30)

  Combining vector norm (Equation 31):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ} = pвӮ– П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)        ... (Eq. 31)

  Note: Eqs. (30) and (31) are identical! This is a special property of MR
  combining.

  Interference power (Equation 32):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} = pвӮ– П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(**

в—Ҹ Now I have all the context. Here is the comprehensive Section V-B explanation.

  ---
  SECTION V-B: UPLINK DATA TRANSMISSION (SCALABLE FRAMEWORK)

  Paper: "Scalable Cell-Free Massive MIMO Systems" вҖ” BjГ¶rnson & Sanguinetti 
  (2020)

  (Second part of Section V. Covers centralized combining (V-B1) and distributed
   combining (V-B2).)

  ---
  1. HIGH-LEVEL EXPLANATION (Layman's Terms)

  Now that the clusters are formed (Section V-A), the actual data communication
  begins. This section focuses on the uplink вҖ” when the users (phones) send data
   to the access points (APs).

  Imagine many people at a cocktail party all talking simultaneously. Each small
   microphone (AP) picks up a mixture of all voices. The challenge: extract one 
  specific person's voice from the mix. This is called receive combining вҖ”
  mathematically weighting the signals from different microphones to amplify the
   desired speaker and suppress others.

  There are two fundamentally different ways to organize this:

  Centralized (Level 4): All microphones send their raw recordings to a master
  sound engineer (CPU). The engineer, having all recordings, can optimally
  separate voices. This gives the best quality, but requires sending massive
  amounts of data to the engineer (high fronthaul).

  Distributed (Level 3): Each microphone has a local processor that makes a best
   guess about what each speaker said. Only these guesses (not the raw
  recordings) are sent to the engineer, who combines them. Less data travels to
  the engineer (low fronthaul), but each local processor sees only part of the
  picture.

  The key innovation in this section: New combining schemes (P-MMSE and LP-MMSE)
   that are nearly as good as the best possible combining but with bounded, 
  scalable complexity.

  ---
  2. DETAILED TECHNICAL EXPLANATION (PhD Level)

  2.1 Two Levels of Cooperation

  The paper considers two levels of cooperation among APs, inspired by [7]:

  Level 1 вҖ” Centralized Combining (Section V-B1):
  - Each AP l sends its raw pilot signals {yвӮңвӮ—бө–вҒұЛЎбө’бө— : t = 1,...,П„вӮҡ} and raw data
   signal yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ to the CPU via fronthaul
  - The CPU performs all processing: channel estimation + data detection
  - Fronthaul load per AP per coherence block: П„вӮҡN + П„бөӨN complex scalars (see
  Table I)
  - The CPU has access to all channel estimates from the serving APs вҶ’ can do
  joint processing

  Level 2 вҖ” Distributed Combining (Section V-B2):
  - Each AP l locally estimates channels {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—} and computes local soft
  estimates vвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ
  - Only these soft estimates (scalars) are sent to CPU for final decoding
  - Fronthaul load per AP per coherence block: П„бөӨ|рқ’ҹвӮ—| complex scalars (see Table
   I)
  - Much lower fronthaul, but each AP processes in isolation

  Fronthaul comparison (Table I):

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ     Signal      в”Ӯ Centralized в”Ӯ      Distributed      в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Pilot signals   в”Ӯ П„вӮҡN per AP  в”Ӯ вҖ” (processed locally) в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ UL data signals в”Ӯ П„бөӨN per AP  в”Ӯ П„бөӨ|рқ’ҹвӮ—| per AP         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ DL data signals в”Ӯ П„_dN per AP в”Ӯ П„_d|рқ’ҹвӮ—| per AP        в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  For the centralized case, the fronthaul load is proportional to N (antennas
  per AP), independent of which UEs are served. For the distributed case, it is
  proportional to |рқ’ҹвӮ—| вүӨ П„вӮҡ, independent of N. With Assumption 1, the
  distributed fronthaul is bounded by П„бөӨП„вӮҡ вҖ” scalable.

  ---
  2.2 SECTION V-B1: CENTRALIZED COMBINING

  2.2.1 Proposition 1 вҖ” Achievable UL SE (Centralized)

  When the CPU has access to the MMSE channel estimates, an achievable SE for UE
   k is:

  в–Һ SEвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = (П„бөӨ/П„б¶ң) В· рқ”ј{logвӮӮ(1 + SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ)}        ... (Eq. 17)

  where the instantaneous effective SINR is:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = pвӮ–|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ / (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· pбөў|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘбөў|ВІ + vвӮ–бҙҙ ZвӮ– vвӮ–)       
   ... (Eq. 18)

  with:

  в–Һ ZвӮ– = DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў Cбөў + ПғВІбөӨвӮ— IвӮ—вӮҷ) DвӮ–

  Let me unpack each component:

  Numerator вҖ” pвӮ–|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ:
  - This is the desired signal power after combining
  - DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– keeps only the estimates from APs serving UE k (zeroes out the rest)
  - vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– is the inner product between the combining vector and the known
  part of the desired channel
  - Squared magnitude gives signal power

  Denominator вҖ” first term вҖ” вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘбөў|ВІ:
  - Interference from estimated components of other UEs' channels
  - These terms are known to the CPU (it has the estimates) and can potentially
  be suppressed by choosing vвӮ– wisely

  Denominator вҖ” second term вҖ” vвӮ–бҙҙ ZвӮ– vвӮ–:
  - Residual interference + noise from channel estimation errors
  - Cбөў = diag(CбөўвӮҒ,...,CбөўвӮ—) is the error covariance of UE i's channel estimate
  - вҲ‘бөў pбөў Cбөў represents the total power of estimation errors from all UEs
  - ПғВІбөӨвӮ— IвӮ—вӮҷ is the noise power
  - DвӮ– sandwiches everything because only serving APs contribute

  Why is this called "instantaneous" SINR? Because it depends on the specific
  channel estimate realizations {ДҘбөў} вҖ” not just statistics. The expectation рқ”ј{В·}
   in Eq. (17) averages over all possible channel realizations.

  Where does Proposition 1 come from? It follows the proof of [2, Theorem 4.1]
  for Massive MIMO. The key idea: given the channel estimates, the CPU knows the
   effective channels vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘбөў and can compute the SINR. The remaining
  uncertainty (estimation errors) is treated as Gaussian noise вҖ” a standard
  capacity lower bound.

  Generality: The expression holds for any combining vector vвӮ–, any spatial
  correlation matrices, any DCC selection, and any number N of AP antennas. It
  subsumes all previous results [7], [30], [47], [48] as special cases.

  2.2.2 Partial Channel Knowledge at the CPU

  An important subtlety: the CPU can only partially compute the collective
  estimate. Only APs in в„івӮ– send their pilot signals, so the CPU knows:

  в–Һ Dбөў ДҘбөў = [DбөўвӮҒ ДҘбөўвӮҒбөҖ  ...  DбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бөҖ]бөҖ        ... (Eq. 16)

  Unknown estimates (from APs not serving UE i) are represented by zeros. The
  distribution is:

  в–Һ Dбөў ДҘбөў ~ рқ’©б¶ң(0, pбөўП„вӮҡ Dбөў Rбөў ОЁвӮңбөўвҒ»В№ Rбөў Dбөў)

  where ОЁвӮңбөўвҒ»В№ = diag(ОЁвӮңбөўвӮҒвҒ»В№,...,ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№).

  2.2.3 MR Combining (Equation 19)

  The simplest centralized combining choice:

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙ№бҙҝ = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 19)

  This just uses the known channel estimate, gated by the DCC matrix. It
  maximizes the numerator |vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–|ВІ of Eq. (18) but ignores the denominator.

  Computational complexity (Table II): Since DвӮ– = diag(DвӮ–вӮҒ,...,DвӮ–вӮ—) and DвӮ–вӮ— = 0вӮҷ
   when l вҲү в„івӮ–, only estimates ДҘвӮ–вӮ— with l вҲҲ в„івӮ– are needed. No matrix inversions
  вҖ” just picking the right estimates. MR complexity is O(NП„вӮҡ + NВІ) per UE for
  channel estimation, and zero additional cost for computing the combining
  vector itself.

  2.2.4 MMSE Combining вҖ” Optimal but Unscalable (Equation 20)

  The SINR in Eq. (18) has the form of a generalized Rayleigh quotient with
  respect to vвӮ–:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ– = (vвӮ–бҙҙ a)(aбҙҙ vвӮ–) / (vвӮ–бҙҙ B vвӮ–)

  where a = вҲҡpвӮ– DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– and B = вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–.

  The Rayleigh quotient is a fundamental concept in linear algebra. For
  Hermitian matrices, the ratio vбҙҙ A v / vбҙҙ B v is maximized by the generalized
  eigenvector corresponding to the largest generalized eigenvalue of (A, B).
  When A is rank-1 (A = a aбҙҙ), the maximizer is simply:

  в–Һ vвӮ’вӮҡвӮң = BвҒ»В№ a

  This gives the MMSE combining vector (Corollary 1):

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 20)

  where (В·)вҖ  denotes the pseudo-inverse (used instead of regular inverse because
   ZвӮ– may not be strictly positive definite).

  The maximum SINR achieved by MMSE combining (Corollary 1):

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'В№вҒҫ = pвӮ– ДҘвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... 
  (Eq. 21)

  Physical interpretation of MMSE combining: The matrix (вҲ‘бөў pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– +
  ZвӮ–)вҖ  is the inverse of the interference-plus-noise covariance (conditioned on
  channel estimates). Pre-multiplying by this matrix "whitens" the interference
  вҖ” it transforms the received signal so that all interference and noise have
  equal, unit variance. Then the inner product with DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– projects onto the
  desired channel direction. This is exactly the Wiener filter.

  The MSE connection (stated after Corollary 1): The MMSE combiner also
  minimizes:

  в–Һ MSEвӮ– = рқ”ј{|sвӮ– вҲ’ ЕқвӮ–|ВІ | {ДҘбөў}}

  the conditional mean squared error between the transmitted signal sвӮ– and the
  decoded signal ЕқвӮ– вҖ” hence the name "MMSE."

  WHY MMSE IS UNSCALABLE: Equation (20) requires computing all K channel
  estimates {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i = 1,...,K} at every AP l вҲҲ в„івӮ–. The matrix to invert has
  dimensions (N|в„івӮ–|) Г— (N|в„івӮ–|), but more critically, the sum has K terms вҖ”
  growing with the number of UEs. Complexity per UE from Table II:

  в–Һ (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ + (N|в„івӮ–|)/2 В· K + (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ + (N|в„івӮ–|)Ві вҲ’ (N|в„івӮ–|)/3

  The K in the second term makes this unscalable.

  2.2.5 P-MMSE Combining вҖ” The Scalable Innovation (Equation 23)

  The key insight from [30]: the interference affecting UE k is mainly generated
   by a small subset of other UEs вҖ” specifically, those served by partially the 
  same APs as UE k. Define:

  в–Һ рқ’«вӮ– = {i : DвӮ– Dбөў вү  0вӮ—вӮҷ}        ... (Eq. 22)

  This is the set of UEs whose cooperation clusters overlap with UE k's cluster.
   If UE i has no shared APs with UE k (DвӮ– Dбөў = 0), then UE i's estimated
  channel contribution DвӮ– ДҘбөў is zero at the APs serving UE k, meaning its
  interference cannot be suppressed anyway.

  The P-MMSE combining vector:

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + Z'вӮ–)вҖ  DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–        ... (Eq. 23)

  with:

  в–Һ Z'вӮ– = DвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮ– pбөў Cбөў + ПғВІбөӨвӮ— IвӮ—вӮҷ) DвӮ–        ... (Eq. 24)

  Key differences from full MMSE:
  1. The sum is over рқ’«вӮ– (not all K UEs) вҖ” bounded number of terms
  2. Z'вӮ– also sums over рқ’«вӮ– only

  Why is |рқ’«вӮ–| bounded?

  Under Assumption 1 (at most one UE per pilot per AP):

  - If all APs serving UE k communicate with exactly the same set of UEs: |рқ’«вӮ–| =
   П„вӮҡ
  - Worst case: all APs in в„івӮ– serve UE k but otherwise serve entirely different
  UEs:
  в–Һ |рқ’«вӮ–| вүӨ (П„вӮҡ вҲ’ 1)|в„івӮ–| + 1

  Both bounds are independent of K вҶ’ P-MMSE is scalable вң…

  When P-MMSE equals full MMSE: When UE k is served by all APs (original
  Cell-Free, Dбөў = IвӮҳ for all i), then рқ’«вӮ– = {1,...,K} and P-MMSE reduces to full
  MMSE. So P-MMSE is a generalization that becomes exact in the unscalable case.

  Computational complexity (from Table II):

  в–Һ Channel estimation: (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ)|рқ’«вӮ–||в„івӮ–|
  в–Һ Combining vector: (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ+(N|в„івӮ–|)/2 В· |рқ’«вӮ–| + (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ + (N|в„івӮ–|)Ві вҲ’ 
  (N|в„івӮ–|)/3

  Everything depends on |рқ’«вӮ–| and |в„івӮ–| (both bounded), not on K вҶ’ scalable.

  ---
  2.3 SECTION V-B2: DISTRIBUTED COMBINING

  2.3.1 The Distributed Processing Model

  Instead of sending raw signals to the CPU, each AP l:
  1. Locally selects combining vectors vвӮ–вӮ— using its local estimates {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ
  рқ’ҹвӮ—}
  2. Computes the local soft estimate of sвӮ–:

  в–Һ ЕқвӮ–вӮ— = vвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ DвӮ–вӮ— yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ        ... (Eq. 25)

  3. Sends ЕқвӮ–вӮ— (a single complex scalar) to the CPU

  The CPU forms the final estimate by summing local estimates from all serving
  APs:

  в–Һ ЕқвӮ– = вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё ЕқвӮ–вӮ—        ... (Eq. 26)

  Fronthaul per AP: AP l sends |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars per UL time slot. Over one coherence
   block: П„бөӨ|рқ’ҹвӮ—| complex scalars. Upper bounded by П„бөӨП„вӮҡ вҖ” scalable, does not
  grow with K.

  2.3.2 Proposition 2 вҖ” Achievable UL SE (Distributed)

  Since the CPU does not have access to channel estimates in the distributed
  case, the SE cannot be computed as in Proposition 1. Instead, the paper uses
  the Use-and-then-Forget (UatF) bound:

  в–Һ SEвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ = (П„бөӨ/П„б¶ң) В· logвӮӮ(1 + SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ)        ... (Eq. 27)

  Note: the logвӮӮ is outside the expectation (no рқ”ј{В·} around the log), unlike
  Proposition 1. This is because the bound is based on statistical SINR, not
  instantaneous.

  The SINR is:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ = pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ / (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} вҲ’ pвӮ–|рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– 
  hвӮ–}|ВІ + ПғВІбөӨвӮ— рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ})        ... (Eq. 28)

  Let me carefully decompose each term:

  Numerator вҖ” pвӮ– |рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ:
  - The mean effective channel рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–} is treated as the known,
  deterministic part of the signal
  - This is the "use" part вҖ” we used the channel estimate to design vвӮ–, then we
  "forget" it
  - The UE only needs to know this average value (learnable over many coherence
  blocks)
  - Squaring gives the power of the deterministic signal component

  Denominator вҖ” first part вҖ” вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ}:
  - Total average power from ALL UEs (including desired UE k)

  Denominator вҖ” second part вҖ” subtract pвӮ–|рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–}|ВІ:
  - Removes the deterministic signal component (already in numerator)
  - What remains: variance of the desired channel + all interference powers

  Denominator вҖ” third part вҖ” ПғВІбөӨвӮ— рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ}:
  - Noise term, amplified by the combining vector's norm

  The denominator can be rewritten as:

  в–Һ pвӮ– Var{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–} + вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} + ПғВІбөӨвӮ— рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ}

  which reveals: desired channel uncertainty + multi-user interference + noise.

  Why the UatF bound? In distributed processing, the CPU does not know the
  instantaneous effective channel vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–. It only knows the mean рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ–
  hвӮ–}. The deviation from the mean is treated as additional noise вҖ” worst-case
  uncorrelated Gaussian noise. This gives a conservative but achievable SE.

  2.3.3 MR Combining вҖ” Closed-Form Results (Corollary 2)

  With MR combining vвӮ–вӮ— = ДҘвӮ–вӮ—, all expectations in Proposition 2 can be computed
   in closed form:

  Mean effective channel (Eq. 30):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hвӮ–} = pвӮ–П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)

  Combining vector norm (Eq. 31):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮ– vвӮ–вҖ–ВІ} = pвӮ–П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)

  Interference power (Eq. 32):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{|vвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– hбөў|ВІ} = pвӮ–П„вӮҡ вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RбөўвӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)

  plus a pilot contamination term (only when UE i shares the same pilot as UE k,
   i.e., tбөў = tвӮ–):

  в–Һ - pвӮ– pбөў П„вӮҡВІ |вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RбөўвӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)|ВІ

  This last term is the coherent pilot contamination interference вҖ” it only
  exists between co-pilot UEs and can scale with N, making it particularly
  harmful.

  2.3.4 LP-MMSE Combining вҖ” The Scalable Distributed Scheme (Equation 29)

  The paper proposes Local Partial MMSE (LP-MMSE) combining:

  в–Һ vвӮ–вӮ—бҙёбҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ)вҒ»В№ ДҘвӮ–вӮ—        ... (Eq. 
  29)

  Let me carefully unpack this:

  The matrix being inverted: вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ

  This has three components:
  - ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ: the estimated channel outer product (known interference structure)
  - CбөўвӮ—: the estimation error covariance (unknown interference from estimation
  errors)
  - ПғВІ IвӮҷ: thermal noise

  Together: вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) = вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў рқ”ј{hбөўвӮ— hбөўвӮ—бҙҙ | ДҘбөўвӮ—} since for
  MMSE estimation:

  в–Һ рқ”ј{hбөўвӮ— hбөўвӮ—бҙҙ | ДҘбөўвӮ—} = ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—

  So the matrix represents the conditional covariance of the total received 
  signal at AP l, given the channel estimates.

  Key difference from L-MMSE [7]: L-MMSE sums over all K UEs; LP-MMSE sums only
  over рқ’ҹвӮ— (at most П„вӮҡ UEs). This is what makes it scalable.

  The matrix dimension: N Г— N (only the local AP's antennas). This is
  dramatically smaller than P-MMSE's N|в„івӮ–| Г— N|в„івӮ–| matrix.

  Computational complexity (from Table II):

  в–Һ Per AP l: NВІ + N/2 В· |рқ’ҹвӮ—| + NВівҲ’N/3 + NВІ per UE served

  The cubic term NВі comes from the N Г— N matrix inversion. Since both N and |рқ’ҹвӮ—|
   вүӨ П„вӮҡ are constants:

  в–Һ Complexity per AP = O(1) as K вҶ’ вҲһ вң…

  Why LP-MMSE vastly outperforms MR: LP-MMSE does two things MR cannot:
  1. Suppresses interference spatially if N > 1: It uses the N-dimensional
  antenna space to steer nulls toward interfering UEs served by the same AP
  2. Reduces channel gain variations: The effective channel hвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ wвӮ–вӮ— has more
  concentrated statistics, improving the SE bound tightness (this is the
  phenomenon illustrated in Fig. 4 of the paper)

  ---
  3. HISTORICAL CONTEXT AND PRIOR DEVELOPMENTS

  3.1 Combining Schemes in Massive MIMO вҖ” Evolution

  3.2 The Generalized Rayleigh Quotient вҖ” Mathematical Foundation

  The Rayleigh quotient dates back to Lord Rayleigh (1877) for vibrating
  systems. In matrix theory:

  в–Һ For Hermitian A and positive definite B, the ratio R(v) = vбҙҙ A v / vбҙҙ B v 
  is:
  в–Һ - Maximized by v = BвҒ»В№ a when A = a aбҙҙ (rank-1)
  в–Һ - Maximum value: aбҙҙ BвҒ»В№ a

  This is [2, Lemma B.10] in the Massive MIMO monograph, which directly yields
  Corollary 1.

  3.3 The UatF Bound вҖ” History

  The Use-and-then-Forget bounding technique:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ Year в”Ӯ            Development             в”Ӯ           Source            в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

  The name "use-and-then-forget" comes from the two-step process: "use" the
  channel estimate to design the combiner, then "forget" it for the SE
  computation (treat the effective channel as deterministic).

  ---
  4. MATHEMATICAL DEEP DIVE

  4.1 Proving MMSE Combining Maximizes SINR вҖ” The Rayleigh Quotient

  The instantaneous SINR (Eq. 18) can be written as:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ– = vвӮ–бҙҙ (pвӮ– DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– ДҘвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ–) vвӮ– / vвӮ–бҙҙ (вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–) vвӮ–

  Define:
  - A = pвӮ– DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– ДҘвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– (rank-1, positive semidefinite)
  - B = вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ– (interference + noise covariance)

  Then SINRвӮ– = vвӮ–бҙҙ A vвӮ– / vвӮ–бҙҙ B vвӮ– is a generalized Rayleigh quotient.

  Since A is rank-1 (A = pвӮ– a aбҙҙ where a = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–):

  в–Һ max_v vбҙҙ a aбҙҙ v / vбҙҙ B v = aбҙҙ BвҒ»В№ a

  achieved by v = BвҒ»В№ a (up to a scalar). Substituting:

  в–Һ vвӮ–бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = (вҲ‘бөўвү вӮ– pбөў DвӮ– ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮ– + ZвӮ–)вҒ»В№ DвӮ– ДҘвӮ–

  which equals Eq. (20) up to the scalar pвӮ–.

  4.2 P-MMSE: Why Only рқ’«вӮ– Matters

  Consider UE i with рқ’ҹвӮ– вҲ© в„ібөў = вҲ… (no shared APs with UE k). Then:

  в–Һ DвӮ– Dбөў = 0 вҶ’ DвӮ– ДҘбөў = DвӮ– Dбөў ДҘбөў = 0

  Wait вҖ” more precisely, DвӮ–вӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ— is only nonzero when both DвӮ–вӮ— = IвӮҷ and ДҘбөўвӮ— вү  0.
   The estimate ДҘбөўвӮ— is generally nonzero for all l (even if AP l doesn't serve
  UE i, the MMSE estimate at AP l of UE i's channel is nonzero due to pilot
  contamination).

  Actually, the key point is: under the DCC framework, AP l only computes ДҘбөўвӮ— 
  for i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—. If i вҲү рқ’ҹвӮ—, AP l does not compute ДҘбөўвӮ— вҖ” it effectively treats it as
   zero. So:

  в–Һ If i вҲү рқ’ҹвӮ— for all l вҲҲ в„івӮ– вҶ’ DвӮ– ДҘбөў = 0 вҶ’ UE i contributes nothing to Eq. (20)

  The set of UEs whose estimated channels are nonzero at the APs serving UE k
  is:

  в–Һ рқ’«вӮ– = {i : DвӮ– Dбөў вү  0вӮ—вӮҷ} = {i : вҲғ l вҲҲ в„івӮ– such that i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—}

  Bounding |рқ’«вӮ–|: Each AP l вҲҲ в„івӮ– serves at most П„вӮҡ UEs (Assumption 1). One of
  them is UE k. So each AP contributes at most (П„вӮҡ вҲ’ 1) other UEs to рқ’«вӮ–. Over
  |в„івӮ–| APs:

  в–Һ |рқ’«вӮ–| вүӨ (П„вӮҡ вҲ’ 1)|в„івӮ–| + 1

  If all APs in в„івӮ– serve exactly the same UEs (maximally overlapping clusters):
  |рқ’«вӮ–| = П„вӮҡ.

  4.3 LP-MMSE: Deriving Equation (29)

  At AP l, the local received signal is:

  в–Һ yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ = вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· hбөўвӮ— sбөў + nвӮ—

  The local MMSE estimate of sвӮ– (given local CSI) seeks the vector vвӮ–вӮ— that
  minimizes:

  в–Һ рқ”ј{|sвӮ– вҲ’ vвӮ–вӮ—бҙҙ yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ|ВІ | {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—}}

  The solution (local Wiener filter):

  в–Һ vвӮ–вӮ— = рқ”ј{yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ (yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ)бҙҙ | {ДҘбөўвӮ—}}вҒ»В№ В· рқ”ј{yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ sвӮ–* | {ДҘбөўвӮ—}}

  The cross-correlation: рқ”ј{yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ sвӮ–*} = pвӮ– hвӮ–вӮ—, and after conditioning on the
  estimate: рқ”ј{hвӮ–вӮ— | ДҘвӮ–вӮ—} = ДҘвӮ–вӮ—.

  The auto-correlation: рқ”ј{yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ (yвӮ—бөҳЛЎ)бҙҙ | {ДҘбөўвӮ—}} = вҲ‘бөў pбөў рқ”ј{hбөўвӮ— hбөўвӮ—бҙҙ | ДҘбөўвӮ—} + ПғВІ
  IвӮҷ

  For i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ— (known UEs):
  в–Һ рқ”ј{hбөўвӮ— hбөўвӮ—бҙҙ | ДҘбөўвӮ—} = ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—

  For i вҲү рқ’ҹвӮ— (unknown UEs): AP l has no estimate вҶ’ contributes only through
  statistics. The LP-MMSE simplification drops these terms (only includes i вҲҲ
  рқ’ҹвӮ—), yielding Eq. (29):

  в–Һ vвӮ–вӮ—бҙёбҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ = pвӮ– (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў (ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮҷ)вҒ»В№ ДҘвӮ–вӮ—

  This is an N Г— N matrix inversion вҖ” O(NВі) per AP, independent of K.

  4.4 Complexity Comparison (Table II Decoded)

  For a generic UE k served by |в„івӮ–| APs:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ Scheme  в”Ӯ  Channel estimation  в”Ӯ   Combining computation    в”Ӯ Scalable? в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ MR      в”Ӯ (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ)|в„івӮ–|       в”Ӯ 0 (just use ДҘвӮ–вӮ—)           в”Ӯ вң…        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ MMSE    в”Ӯ (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ)K|в„івӮ–|      в”Ӯ O((N|в„івӮ–|)Ві + (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІK)    в”Ӯ вқҢ        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ P-MMSE  в”Ӯ (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ)|рқ’«вӮ–||в„івӮ–|   в”Ӯ O((N|в„івӮ–|)Ві + (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ|рқ’«вӮ–|) в”Ӯ вң…        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ LP-MMSE в”Ӯ (NП„вӮҡ + NВІ)вҲ‘вӮ—вҲҲв„івӮ– |рқ’ҹвӮ—| в”Ӯ O(NВі|в„івӮ–|)                  в”Ӯ вң…        в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  The bold K in MMSE row is the scalability-breaker. P-MMSE and LP-MMSE replace
  K with bounded quantities.

  ---
  5. NUMERICAL EXAMPLES

  Example 1: MR vs P-MMSE vs LP-MMSE вҖ” SINR Comparison

  Setup: L = 4 APs, N = 2, K = 3, П„вӮҡ = 3. AP l serves UEs: рқ’ҹвӮҒ = {1,2}, рқ’ҹвӮӮ =
  {1,3}, рқ’ҹвӮғ = {2,3}, рқ’ҹвӮ„ = {3}.

  UE 1's cluster: в„івӮҒ = {1, 2}. Overlapping UEs: рқ’«вӮҒ = {1, 2, 3} (UE 2 via AP 1,
  UE 3 via AP 2).

  Channel estimates at APs serving UE 1 (N = 2):

  ДҘвӮҒвӮҒ = [0.5, 0.3]бөҖ,  ДҘвӮӮвӮҒ = [0.1, вҲ’0.2]бөҖ     (AP 1)
  ДҘвӮҒвӮӮ = [0.4, 0.1]бөҖ,  ДҘвӮғвӮӮ = [вҲ’0.1, 0.3]бөҖ     (AP 2)
  Error covariances (simplified): CбөўвӮ— = 0.001 IвӮӮ for all i,l. ПғВІ = 0.01, pбөў =
  0.1 for all i.

  MR combining: vвӮҒ = DвӮҒ ДҘвӮҒ = [ДҘвӮҒвӮҒбөҖ  ДҘвӮҒвӮӮбөҖ]бөҖ = [0.5, 0.3, 0.4, 0.1]бөҖ

  Desired signal power (numerator of SINR):
  в–Һ |vвӮҒбҙҙ DвӮҒ ДҘвӮҒ|ВІ = |[0.5, 0.3, 0.4, 0.1] В· [0.5, 0.3, 0.4, 0.1]бөҖ|ВІ = 
  |0.25+0.09+0.16+0.01|ВІ = |0.51|ВІ = 0.260

  MR ignores interference entirely. The SINR will be limited by whatever
  interference leaks through.

  P-MMSE combining: Would invert the 4Г—4 matrix:
  в–Һ B = вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’«вӮҒ pбөў DвӮҒ ДҘбөў ДҘбөўбҙҙ DвӮҒ + Z'вӮҒ

  This matrix accounts for UEs 2 and 3's estimated channels and actively
  suppresses them.

  LP-MMSE combining: Each AP inverts a 2Г—2 matrix independently:

  At AP 1: BвӮҒ = 0.1([0.5,0.3]бөҖ[0.5,0.3] + 0.001IвӮӮ) + 0.1([0.1,вҲ’0.2]бөҖ[0.1,вҲ’0.2] +
   0.001IвӮӮ) + 0.01IвӮӮ

  в–Һ = 0.1[0.25,0.15; 0.15,0.09] + 0.1[0.01,вҲ’0.02; вҲ’0.02,0.04] + 0.1Г—0.001IвӮӮГ—2 + 
  0.01IвӮӮ

  The inversion of this 2Г—2 matrix allows AP 1 to partially suppress UE 2's
  interference.

  Example 2: Fronthaul Comparison

  Setup: L = 100 APs, N = 4, П„вӮҡ = 10, П„бөӨ = 190, П„_d = 190. |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 8 UEs per AP
  on average.

  Centralized fronthaul per AP per coherence block:
  в–Һ Pilot: П„вӮҡ Г— N = 10 Г— 4 = 40 complex scalars
  в–Һ UL data: П„бөӨ Г— N = 190 Г— 4 = 760 complex scalars
  в–Һ Total UL: 40 + 760 = 800 complex scalars

  Distributed fronthaul per AP per coherence block:
  в–Һ Pilot: 0 (processed locally)
  в–Һ UL data: П„бөӨ Г— |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 190 Г— 8 = 1,520 complex scalars

  Wait вҖ” in this case distributed is actually more for UL data! This is because
  N = 4 < |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 8. Let me recalculate: the centralized case sends N-dimensional
   vectors (4 scalars per time slot), while distributed sends |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars (8
  per time slot).

  For N = 4, |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 8: Distributed requires more fronthaul for UL data.
  For N = 8, |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 4: Distributed requires less fronthaul.

  Key insight: Distributed saves fronthaul when N > |рқ’ҹвӮ—|, which occurs with
  many-antenna APs. With single-antenna APs (N = 1), distributed always saves: 1
   scalar (centralized) vs. |рқ’ҹвӮ—| scalars (distributed) per time slot вҖ” wait,
  that's also more for distributed.

  Actually the comparison is: centralized sends N per slot (raw signal);
  distributed sends |рқ’ҹвӮ—| per slot (one scalar per UE). So distributed saves when
   |рқ’ҹвӮ—| < N. The advantage of distributed is no pilot signals on fronthaul
  (saving П„вӮҡN scalars) and potentially lower total if |рқ’ҹвӮ—| is small relative to
  N.

  Example 3: |рқ’«вӮ–| Computation

  Setup: П„вӮҡ = 5, UE k is served by |в„івӮ–| = 3 APs.

  Best case: All 3 APs serve exactly the same 5 UEs:
  в–Һ рқ’«вӮ– = those 5 UEs вҶ’ |рқ’«вӮ–| = 5 = П„вӮҡ

  Worst case: Each AP serves UE k + 4 unique other UEs:
  в–Һ AP 1: {k, aвӮҒ, aвӮӮ, aвӮғ, aвӮ„}
  в–Һ AP 2: {k, bвӮҒ, bвӮӮ, bвӮғ, bвӮ„}
  в–Һ AP 3: {k, cвӮҒ, cвӮӮ, cвӮғ, cвӮ„}
  в–Һ рқ’«вӮ– = {k, aвӮҒ,...,aвӮ„, bвӮҒ,...,bвӮ„, cвӮҒ,...,cвӮ„} вҶ’ |рқ’«вӮ–| = 1 + 3Г—4 = 13

  Bound: (П„вӮҡвҲ’1)|в„івӮ–| + 1 = 4Г—3 + 1 = 13 вң“

  In either case, |рқ’«вӮ–| вүӨ 13, independent of K. If K = 10,000, the P-MMSE
  combiner still only considers at most 13 UEs.

  ---
  6. PRACTICE PROBLEMS

  Problem 1: UatF Bound Computation

  Consider a distributed Cell-Free system with L = 2 APs, N = 1 (single
  antenna), K = 2 UEs on different pilots. MR combining (vвӮ–вӮ— = ДҘвӮ–вӮ—). Perfect
  estimation (no contamination).

  Channel statistics: рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮҒ|ВІ} = ОІвӮҒвӮҒ = 0.01, рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮӮ|ВІ} = ОІвӮҒвӮӮ = 0.005.
  pвӮҒ = pвӮӮ = 0.1 W, ПғВІ = 10вҒ»Ві W.

  (a) Compute the mean effective channel for UE 1: рқ”ј{vвӮҒбҙҙ DвӮҒ hвӮҒ}
  (b) Compute рқ”ј{|vвӮҒбҙҙ DвӮҒ hвӮҒ|ВІ}
  (c) Compute SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ for UE 1 (assume UE 2 creates no interference due to
  different pilot and MR combining)

  Solutions:

  (a) With MR and no contamination (Eq. 30 simplified for N = 1):
  в–Һ рқ”ј{vвӮҒбҙҙ DвӮҒ hвӮҒ} = рқ”ј{ДҘвӮҒвӮҒ* hвӮҒвӮҒ + ДҘвӮҒвӮӮ* hвӮҒвӮӮ}
  в–Һ = рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮҒ|ВІ} + рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮӮ|ВІ}  (since ДҘвӮ–вӮ— = hвӮ–вӮ— for perfect estimation)
  в–Һ = ОІвӮҒвӮҒ + ОІвӮҒвӮӮ = 0.01 + 0.005 = 0.015

  (b) рқ”ј{|vвӮҒбҙҙ DвӮҒ hвӮҒ|ВІ} = рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮҒhвӮҒвӮҒ + ДҘвӮҒвӮӮhвӮҒвӮӮ|ВІ}
  в–Һ = рқ”ј{|hвӮҒвӮҒ|вҒҙ} + рқ”ј{|hвӮҒвӮӮ|вҒҙ} + 2рқ”ј{|hвӮҒвӮҒ|ВІ}рқ”ј{|hвӮҒвӮӮ|ВІ}
  в–Һ For CN(0, ОІ): рқ”ј{|h|вҒҙ} = 2ОІВІ
  в–Һ = 2(0.01)ВІ + 2(0.005)ВІ + 2Г—0.01Г—0.005 = 2Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ + 5Г—10вҒ»вҒө + 10вҒ»вҒҙ = 3.5Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ

  (c) Denominator of Eq. (28) (assuming negligible UE 2 interference):
  в–Һ pвӮҒ(рқ”ј{|vвӮҒбҙҙDвӮҒhвӮҒ|ВІ} вҲ’ |рқ”ј{vвӮҒбҙҙDвӮҒhвӮҒ}|ВІ) + ПғВІрқ”ј{вҖ–DвӮҒvвӮҒвҖ–ВІ}

  Variance term: 0.1 Г— (3.5Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ вҲ’ (0.015)ВІ) = 0.1 Г— (3.5Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ вҲ’ 2.25Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ) =
  0.1 Г— 1.25Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ = 1.25Г—10вҒ»вҒө

  Noise term: 10вҒ»Ві Г— рқ”ј{|ДҘвӮҒвӮҒ|ВІ + |ДҘвӮҒвӮӮ|ВІ} = 10вҒ»Ві Г— 0.015 = 1.5Г—10вҒ»вҒө

  SINR = 0.1 Г— (0.015)ВІ / (1.25Г—10вҒ»вҒө + 1.5Г—10вҒ»вҒө) = 0.1 Г— 2.25Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ / 2.75Г—10вҒ»вҒө =
   2.25Г—10вҒ»вҒө / 2.75Г—10вҒ»вҒө = 0.818 (вҲ’0.87 dB)

  SE = logвӮӮ(1 + 0.818) = logвӮӮ(1.818) = 0.862 bit/s/Hz (before pre-log factor
  П„бөӨ/П„б¶ң)

  Problem 2: P-MMSE Scalability

  A UE k is served by |в„івӮ–| = 4 APs. П„вӮҡ = 10.

  (a) What is the maximum possible |рқ’«вӮ–|?
  (b) If full MMSE requires K = 200 UEs in the sum, how many does P-MMSE need?
  (c) What is the ratio of P-MMSE to MMSE complexity for the combining
  computation (assuming the dominant term is (N|в„івӮ–|)ВІ/2 Г— number of UEs in the
  sum)?

  Solutions:

  (a) |рқ’«вӮ–| вүӨ (П„вӮҡ вҲ’ 1)|в„івӮ–| + 1 = 9 Г— 4 + 1 = 37

  (b) P-MMSE: at most |рқ’«вӮ–| = 37 UEs. Reduction from 200 to 37 = 5.4Г— fewer.

  (c) Complexity ratio вүҲ |рқ’«вӮ–| / K = 37 / 200 = 18.5% of MMSE cost. And
  crucially, this ratio shrinks further as K grows вҖ” at K = 2,000: only 1.85%.

  Problem 3: LP-MMSE Matrix Construction

  AP l has N = 2 antennas, |рқ’ҹвӮ—| = 2 (serves UE 1 and UE 3). pвӮҒ = pвӮғ = 0.1 W, ПғВІ
  = 0.01 W.

  Channel estimates: ДҘвӮҒвӮ— = [0.6, 0.2]бөҖ, ДҘвӮғвӮ— = [вҲ’0.1, 0.5]бөҖ.
  Error covariances: CвӮҒвӮ— = 0.002 IвӮӮ, CвӮғвӮ— = 0.003 IвӮӮ.

  (a) Construct the matrix to invert in Eq. (29) for UE 1.
  (b) What is the dimension of this matrix?
  (c) Compare with full MMSE which would require all K UEs.

  Solutions:

  (a) Matrix = вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— pбөў(ДҘбөўвӮ— ДҘбөўвӮ—бҙҙ + CбөўвӮ—) + ПғВІ IвӮӮ

  = 0.1 Г— ([0.6,0.2]бөҖ[0.6,0.2] + 0.002**I**вӮӮ) + 0.1 Г— ([вҲ’0.1,0.5]бөҖ[вҲ’0.1,0.5] +
  0.003**I**вӮӮ) + 0.01**I**вӮӮ
  First outer product: [0.36, 0.12; 0.12, 0.04]
  Second outer product: [0.01, вҲ’0.05; вҲ’0.05, 0.25]

  = 0.1 Г— [0.362, 0.12; 0.12, 0.042] + 0.1 Г— [0.013, вҲ’0.05; вҲ’0.05, 0.253] +
  [0.01, 0; 0, 0.01]

  = [0.0362, 0.012; 0.012, 0.0042] + [0.0013, вҲ’0.005; вҲ’0.005, 0.0253] + [0.01,
  0; 0, 0.01]

  = **[0.0475, 0.007; 0.007, 0.0395]**
  (b) 2 Г— 2 вҖ” just a tiny matrix! Trivial to invert.

  (c) Full MMSE at the centralized level would require a (N|в„івӮ–|) Г— (N|в„івӮ–|)
  matrix with contributions from all K UEs. If |в„івӮ–| = 4 and K = 200: a 8Г—8
  matrix with 200 outer product terms to sum. LP-MMSE: a 2Г—2 matrix with 2 
  terms. Massive simplification.

  ---
  7. SECTION SUMMARY

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ      Aspect      в”Ӯ                        Detail                        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Two processing   в”Ӯ Centralized (raw signals to CPU) vs. Distributed     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ levels           в”Ӯ (local soft estimates to CPU)                        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Proposition 1    в”Ӯ SE with instantaneous SINR: SINRвӮ– = pвӮ–|vвӮ–бҙҙDвӮ–ДҘвӮ–|ВІ /   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ (interference + errors + noise)                      в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ MR combining     в”Ӯ vвӮ– = DвӮ– ДҘвӮ– вҖ” simple, ignores interference,           в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ closed-form SE                                       в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ MMSE combining   в”Ӯ Maximizes instantaneous SINR via Rayleigh quotient;  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ unscalable (needs all K estimates)                   в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ P-MMSE           в”Ӯ Only includes UEs in рқ’«вӮ– (overlapping clusters); |рқ’«вӮ–| в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  вүӨ (П„вӮҡвҲ’1)|в„івӮ–|+1 вҶ’ scalable                           в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Proposition 2    в”Ӯ UatF bound for distributed: SINR based on            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ statistical expectations, not instantaneous          в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ LP-MMSE          в”Ӯ Local MMSE at each AP; NГ—N inversion only over рқ’ҹвӮ—    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ UEs вҶ’ O(NВі) per AP вҶ’ scalable                        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ LP-MMSE vs MR    в”Ӯ LP-MMSE suppresses interference spatially (N > 1)    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ and reduces channel gain variations                  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Fronthaul        в”Ӯ Centralized: (П„вӮҡ+П„бөӨ)N per AP; Distributed: П„бөӨ|рқ’ҹвӮ—|    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ per AP вҖ” both bounded under DCC                      в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Key innovation   в”Ӯ P-MMSE and LP-MMSE achieve near-MMSE performance     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ with scalable complexity                             в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  ---
  SECTION V-C: DOWNLINK DATA TRANSMISSION (Scalable Precoding)

  Paper: "Scalable Cell-Free Massive MIMO Systems" вҖ” BjГ¶rnson & Sanguinetti 
  (2020)

  (Third part of Section V. Covers Proposition 3 (DL SE), Proposition 4 (UL-DL 
  duality), centralized and distributed precoding, and the channel hardening 
  discussion.)

  ---
  1. HIGH-LEVEL EXPLANATION (Layman's Terms)

  In the uplink (Section V-B), the users talked and the APs listened. Now it's
  the other way around: the APs send data to the users. This is the downlink.

  Precoding is the DL counterpart of combining. When an AP wants to send a
  message to a specific user, it shapes the signal so that it arrives strongly
  at the intended user and weakly at everyone else. This is like a spotlight:
  instead of flooding the room with light (power), you aim a focused beam at one
   person.

  The challenge: In the UL, each UE's combining could be optimized
  independently. In the DL, all precoders are coupled вҖ” changing the precoder
  for one UE affects the interference experienced by all other UEs. Ideally,
  you'd jointly optimize all precoders simultaneously, but that's unscalable.

  The elegant solution вҖ” UL-DL Duality: It turns out that you can design good DL
   precoders by simply reusing the UL combiners! The paper proves (Proposition
  4) that if you set the DL precoding direction equal to the UL combining
  direction, the same SINRs are achievable in the DL (with appropriate power
  adjustment). This is a profound result: it means you never need to explicitly 
  solve the DL precoding problem вҖ” just solve the easier UL combining problem
  and translate the solution.

  Channel hardening is an important subtlety: the DL SE bound assumes the user
  knows only the average effective channel gain (not the instantaneous value).
  This bound is tight when the effective channel is very stable (concentrates
  around its mean) вҖ” which happens with many antennas. With few antennas per AP
  (like N = 1), the bound can be loose, especially with MR precoding. LP-MMSE
  precoding naturally provides much better hardening.

  ---
  2. DETAILED TECHNICAL EXPLANATION (PhD Level)

  2.1 DL Precoding Structure

  The paper assumes the precoding vector for UE i is decomposed as:

  в–Һ wбөў = вҲҡПҒбөў wМ„бөў        ... (Eq. 33)

  where:
  - wМ„бөў вҲҲ в„Ӯбҙ№ determines the spatial directivity of the transmission
  - рқ”ј{вҖ–wМ„бөўвҖ–ВІ} = 1 (unit-norm on average)
  - ПҒбөў вүҘ 0 is the total transmit power allocated to UE i

  This decomposition separates the direction (wМ„бөў) from the power (ПҒбөў), allowing
  them to be designed independently.

  2.2 Proposition 3 вҖ” Achievable DL SE

  The DL SE uses the hardening bound, widely used in Massive MIMO [2, Th. 4.6]
  and in Cell-Free papers [5]вҖ“[7]:

  в–Һ SEвӮ–вҒҪбөҲЛЎвҒҫ = (П„_d/П„б¶ң) В· logвӮӮ(1 + SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҲЛЎвҒҫ)        ... (Eq. 34)

  where:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҲЛЎвҒҫ = ПҒвӮ– |рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wМ„вӮ–}|ВІ / (вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· ПҒбөў рқ”ј{|hвӮ–бҙҙ Dбөў wМ„бөў|ВІ} вҲ’ ПҒвӮ– |рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– 
  wМ„вӮ–}|ВІ + ПғВІ_dl)        ... (Eq. 35)

  Dissecting each component of Eq. (35):

  Numerator вҖ” ПҒвӮ– |рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wМ„вӮ–}|ВІ:
  - рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wМ„вӮ–} is the mean effective channel gain for UE k
  - This is the only thing the UE knows about its channel (it doesn't know the
  instantaneous realization)
  - The UE uses this as a deterministic "channel" for decoding
  - Squared magnitude Г— power ПҒвӮ– gives the useful signal power

  Denominator вҖ” first part вҖ” вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· ПҒбөў рқ”ј{|hвӮ–бҙҙ Dбөў wМ„бөў|ВІ}:
  - Total average received power from ALL UEs (including desired UE k)
  - Includes both the coherent (desired) and non-coherent (interference)
  components
  - Note: Dбөў (not DвӮ–) appears because interference comes from APs serving other
  UEs

  Denominator вҖ” second part вҖ” subtract ПҒвӮ– |рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wМ„вӮ–}|ВІ:
  - Removes the deterministic desired signal power (already in numerator)
  - What remains: variance of the desired channel (channel hardening residual) +
   interference + noise

  Denominator вҖ” third part вҖ” ПғВІ_dl:
  - Receiver noise power at UE k

  The full denominator can be rewritten as:

  в–Һ ПҒвӮ– Var{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wМ„вӮ–} + вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒ,бөўвү вӮ–бҙ· ПҒбөў рқ”ј{|hвӮ–бҙҙ Dбөў wМ„бөў|ВІ} + ПғВІ_dl

  The first term (variance) measures how much the effective channel fluctuates
  around its mean. Small variance вҶ’ strong channel hardening вҶ’ tight bound.
  Large variance вҶ’ weak hardening вҶ’ loose bound.

  Key difference from UL Proposition 2: In the UL (Eq. 28), the SINR depends
  only on vвӮ– (UE k's own combining vector). In the DL (Eq. 35), the SINR depends
   on wМ„бөў for all UEs i вҖ” because the precoding vectors of all UEs collectively
  determine the interference landscape. This coupling makes DL design
  fundamentally harder than UL design.

  2.3 Remark 3 вҖ” When Is the Hardening Bound Tight?

  The paper notes an important caveat (Remark 3): The hardening bound has been
  widely used since the early Massive MIMO papers [22], [53], [54] and is
  reasonable when channel hardening is strong. However:

  - In Cell-Free Massive MIMO with small N (few antennas per AP), hardening can
  be weak [47]
  - The bound depends on the precoding scheme вҖ” LP-MMSE provides much better
  hardening than MR
  - The paper revisits this in Section VI-B with numerical evidence

  Source: Z. Chen and E. BjГ¶rnson, "Channel Hardening and Favorable Propagation
  in Cell-Free Massive MIMO with Stochastic Geometry," IEEE Trans. Commun., vol.
   17, no. 11, 2018 [47].

  2.4 Proposition 4 вҖ” UL-DL Duality (The Key Result)

  This is one of the most elegant results in the paper. It shows that UL
  combining vectors can be directly translated into DL precoding vectors while
  preserving the same SINRs.

  в–Һ Proposition 4: Let {vбөў : i = 1,...,K} and {pбөў : i = 1,...,K} denote the UL 
  combining vectors and transmit powers. If the normalized precoding vectors are
   selected as:

  в–Һ wМ„бөў = vбөў / вҲҡ(рқ”ј{vбөўбҙҙ Dбөў vбөў})        ... (Eq. 36)

  в–Һ then there exists a DL power control policy {ПҒбөў : вҲҖi} with вҲ‘бөў ПҒбөў/ПғВІ_dl = вҲ‘бөў 
  pбөў/ПғВІ_ul for which:

  в–Һ SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҲЛЎвҒҫ = SINRвӮ–вҒҪбөҳЛЎ'ВІвҒҫ    вҲҖk        ... (Eq. 37)

  What this means in plain terms: Take ANY UL combining scheme (MR, P-MMSE,
  LP-MMSE), use the combining vectors as DL precoding directions (after
  normalization), and with the right power allocation, you achieve exactly the 
  same SINRs in the DL as in the UL. The total DL power equals the total UL
  power.

  The normalization in Eq. (36): The denominator вҲҡ(рқ”ј{vбөўбҙҙ Dбөў vбөў}) ensures
  рқ”ј{вҖ–wМ„бөўвҖ–ВІ} = 1, as required by the decomposition in Eq. (33). Note that Dбөў
  appears inside the norm вҖ” only the components of vбөў at APs serving UE i
  contribute.

  The DL power allocation: The paper proves in the Appendix that the DL powers
  are given by:

  в–Һ ПҒ = (О“ вҲ’ ОЈ)вҒ»В№ 1вӮ– ПғВІ_dl        ... (Eq. 48)

  where ПҒ = [ПҒвӮҒ,...,ПҒвӮ–]бөҖ, and О“ and ОЈ are K Г— K matrices defined in terms of the
   effective channels and SINRs. The key result: (О“ вҲ’ ОЈ) is always invertible
  when the UL powers are feasible (which they are by assumption), so the DL
  power solution always exists.

  The total power relation:

  в–Һ вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· ПҒбөў/ПғВІ_dl = вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· pбөў/ПғВІ_ul

  The total DL power (relative to noise) equals the total UL power (relative to
  noise). However, the power is distributed differently across UEs.

  2.5 Why Duality Matters for Scalability

  The DL SINR in Eq. (35) depends on all K precoding vectors {wМ„бөў}. Jointly
  optimizing them is unscalable. But with Proposition 4:

  1. Design UL combining vectors {vбөў} вҖ” can be done per-UE or per-AP (scalable
  schemes exist: P-MMSE, LP-MMSE)
  2. Set wМ„бөў = vбөў / вҲҡ(рқ”ј{vбөўбҙҙ Dбөў vбөў})
  3. If the UL scheme is scalable, the DL scheme is automatically scalable

  This eliminates the need for any DL-specific precoding optimization.

  2.6 Practical Limitation of the Duality

  Despite the theoretical elegance, Proposition 4 has a practical caveat: the DL
   power policy in Eq. (48) requires solving a K Г— K linear system вҖ” unscalable
  complexity. Moreover, UL and DL have different power constraints:
  - UL: per-UE constraint (pбөў вүӨ P for each UE)
  - DL: per-AP constraint (вҲ‘бөўвҲҲрқ’ҹвӮ— рқ”ј{вҖ–wбөўвӮ—вҖ–ВІ} вүӨ ПҒ for each AP)

  The duality result assumes a sum-power constraint, not per-AP constraints. In
  practice, the SE usually differs between UL and DL because the per-AP
  constraints prevent full exploitation of the duality.

  However, the key takeaway remains: Proposition 4 motivates using UL combiners 
  as DL precoders вҖ” and this works well in practice even with heuristic power
  allocation.

  2.7 Centralized Precoding (Section V-C1)

  At the first level of cooperation, the CPU:
  1. Uses UL channel estimates to compute the normalized precoding vectors {wМ„бөўвӮ—}
  2. Exploits channel reciprocity (TDD)
  3. Motivated by UL-DL duality, selects precoding vectors according to Eq. (36)

  By choosing vбөў according to UL combining schemes from V-B1:
  - vбөў = vбөўбҙҫвҒ»бҙ№бҙ№Лўбҙұ вҶ’ P-MMSE precoding
  - vбөў = Dбөў ДҘбөў вҶ’ MR precoding

  Once computed, the CPU forms the DL signal for AP l:

  в–Һ xвӮ—бөҲЛЎ = вҲ‘бөўвӮҢвӮҒбҙ· вҲҡПҒбөў DбөўвӮ— wМ„бөўвӮ— ПӮбөў        ... (Eq. 39)

  and sends this to AP l via fronthaul. The fronthaul load: П„вӮҡN (pilot signals
  from AP to CPU) + П„_dN (DL signals from CPU to AP) complex scalars per
  coherence block (Table I).

  2.8 Distributed Precoding (Section V-C2)

  At the second level, AP l locally selects precoding vectors using only its
  local estimates {ДҘбөўвӮ— : i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—}. The CPU only sends the DL data signals {ПӮбөў : i
   вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—} to AP l. Fronthaul: П„_d|рқ’ҹвӮ—| complex scalars per coherence block вҖ”
  scalable.

  Two scalable distributed precoding schemes:

  MR precoding (conjugate beamforming): wбөўвӮ— вҲқ ДҘбөўвӮ— вҖ” the standard in the
  Cell-Free literature.

  LP-MMSE precoding: Using Eq. (29) from V-B2 as the local combining vector,
  then applying the duality normalization (Eq. 36). This is the first time 
  LP-MMSE precoding is considered in the Cell-Free literature.

  The paper emphasizes the importance of Eq. (38):

  в–Һ DбөўвӮ— wбөўвӮ— = wбөўвӮ—    if i вҲҲ рқ’ҹвӮ—
  в–Һ DбөўвӮ— wбөўвӮ— = 0вӮҷ     if i пҝҪпҝҪпҝҪ рқ’ҹвӮ—        ... (Eq. 38)

  Only the precoding vectors for UEs in рқ’ҹвӮ— need to be computed at AP l. This is
  the mechanism that makes distributed precoding scalable.

  2.9 The LP-MMSE Advantage вҖ” Fig. 4 Analysis

  The paper includes a remarkable result in Fig. 4 that explains why LP-MMSE 
  outperforms MR even in the simplest case (N = L = K = 1, perfect CSI).

  For a single-antenna system with h ~ рқ’©б¶ң(0, 1):

  MR precoding: w = h вҶ’ effective channel gain = hбҙҙw = |h|ВІ. This follows an
  exponential distribution вҖ” it has an infinite tail (large fluctuations, poor
  channel hardening).

  LP-MMSE precoding: w = h / (|h|ВІ + 1/вҲҡ(рқ”ј{|h|ВІ/(|h|ВІ+1)ВІ})). The effective
  channel gain has bounded support вҖ” small, compact distribution (strong
  effective hardening).

  Why this matters for the SE bound: The hardening bound (Proposition 3) treats
  рқ”ј{hбҙҙw} as deterministic. When the actual effective channel hбҙҙw fluctuates
  widely around this mean (MR case), the bound is loose вҖ” it underestimates the
  true capacity. When hбҙҙw concentrates tightly around the mean (LP-MMSE case),
  the bound is tight вҖ” it accurately reflects performance.

  Quantified in Section VI-B: With N = 1 and LP-MMSE, the DL SE achieves 90% of
  a genie-aided case (where the UE knows the instantaneous channel). With MR,
  only 60% is achieved. P-MMSE achieves 98%.

  2.10 Corollary 3 вҖ” Closed-Form DL SE with MR Precoding

  With MR precoding, the expectations in Eq. (35) can be computed in closed
  form:

  Mean effective channel (Eq. 40):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ DвӮ– wвӮ–} = вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё вҲҡПҒбөўвӮ— pвӮ–П„вӮҡ tr(DвӮ–вӮ— RвӮ–вӮ— ОЁвӮңвӮ–вӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—)

  Total interference power (Eq. 41):

  в–Һ рқ”ј{|hвӮ–бҙҙ Dбөў wбөў|ВІ} = вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё ПҒбөўвӮ— tr(DбөўвӮ— RбөўвӮ— ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№ RбөўвӮ— DбөўвӮ— RвӮ–вӮ—) / tr(RбөўвӮ— ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№ 
  RбөўвӮ—)

  в–Һ - (pilot contamination term if tбөў = tвӮ–):
  в–Һ |вҲ‘вӮ—вӮҢвӮҒбҙё вҲҡПҒбөўвӮ— pвӮ–П„вӮҡ tr(DбөўвӮ— RбөўвӮ— ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№ RвӮ–вӮ—) / вҲҡ(tr(RпҝҪпҝҪпҝҪвӮ— ОЁвӮңбөўвӮ—вҒ»В№ RбөўвӮ—))|ВІ

  Note the appearance of ПҒбөўвӮ— (per-AP power for UE i) in the distributed case,
  reflecting the per-AP power allocation from Eq. (43).

  в”Ӯ 2020 в”Ӯ This paper: Proposition 4 extends duality to          в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ      в”Ӯ Cell-Free with DCC                                    в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ 2024 в”Ӯ Miretti & Stanczak: further generalization with       в”Ӯ IEEE TWC  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ      в”Ӯ per-AP information constraints                        в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  The core duality principle: In a multi-user MIMO system, the set of achievable
   SINR tuples in the UL (with sum power P) equals the set of achievable SINR
  tuples in the DL (with sum power P). The UL and DL use the same beamforming 
  directions but different power allocations.

  Why this is profound: The UL is easier to optimize (each UE's combining can be
   optimized independently given other UEs' channels). The duality says: solve
  the easy UL problem, then translate to the hard DL problem вҖ” for free.

  Source: H. Boche and M. Schubert, "A General Duality Theory for Uplink and
  Downlink Beamforming," IEEE VTC-Fall, 2002 [50].

  3.2 Channel Hardening вҖ” Why Cell-Free Is Different

  Channel hardening occurs when the effective channel gain |hвӮ–бҙҙ wвӮ–|ВІ
  concentrates around its mean:

  в–Һ Var{hвӮ–бҙҙ wпҝҪпҝҪпҝҪ} / |рқ”ј{hвӮ–бҙҙ wвӮ–}|ВІ вҶ’ 0

  In co-located Massive MIMO with M antennas and MR precoding:
  в–Һ Var{вҖ–hвӮ–вҖ–ВІ} / (рқ”ј{вҖ–hвӮ–вҖ–ВІ})ВІ = 1/M вҶ’ 0 as M вҶ’ пҝҪпҝҪпҝҪ

  In Cell-Free Massive MIMO: The effective channel is a weighted sum of
  contributions from different APs, each with different pathloss ОІвӮ–вӮ—. The
  hardening depends on the diversity of these weights. If one AP dominates (very
   close to the UE), hardening is weak вҖ” the effective channel is dominated by
  one random variable. If many APs contribute roughly equally, hardening is
  stronger.

  Chen and BjГ¶rnson (2018) [47] showed that hardening in Cell-Free systems is
  generally weaker than in co-located systems, especially with N = 1 antenna per
   AP.

  3.3 Precoding in Cell-Free: Prior Art

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
